–ú–∏–ª–∞ –ì–µ–Ω–¥–µ–ª—å–º–∞–Ω:
The method 'toLowerCase' can't be unconditionally invoked because the receiver can be 'null'. Try making the call conditional (using '?.') or adding a null check to the target ('!').

A nullable expression can't be used as a condition. Try checking that the value isn't 'null' before using it as a condition.
